# InternshipHunter
Data/Tools to consistently be the first to apply to competitive internships

## How to use

``` {.sourceCode .bash}
$ ./FirstToApply 1004 1728 2441 1077
Checking: 23&Me
Checking: Google
Checking: Robinhood
Robinhood application has opened: https://careers.robinhood.com/openings
Checking: AMD
```
